	# COMMUNIST BRANCH
	
		focus = {
		id = HUN_embrace_communism
		icon = GFX_goal_support_communism
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = HUN_revisionism }
		bypass = { 
			has_government = communism
		}
		allow_branch = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_revisionism }
		}
		x = 4
		y = 0
		cost = 5

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL}
		completion_reward = {
			add_stability = -0.2
			add_timed_idea = { idea = spread_of_communism days = 1095 }	
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = turul_movement_start }
		        swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = turul_movement_start
				    add_idea = turul_movement_communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = turul_movement_neutrality }
			    swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = turul_movement_neutrality
				    add_idea = turul_movement_communism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = turul_movement_democratic }
			    swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = turul_movement_democratic
				    add_idea = turul_movement_communism
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = turul_movement_fascism }
			    swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = turul_movement_fascism
				    add_idea = turul_movement_communism		
				}	
			}			
			if = {
			  limit = {
			      has_dlc = "La Resistance"
				}
				create_operative_leader = {
				    name = "András Tömpe"
					GFX = gfx/leaders/HUN/portrait_hun_andras_tompe.dds
					traits = { operative_commando operative_linguist }
					bypass_recruitment = no
	                available_to_spy_master = yes
	                nationalities = { HUN }
				}
			}	
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = HUN_laszlo_rajk
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_government = communism
					is_major = yes
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_leaning_communist }
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism }
					#With realism, most of the claimed territories start as claims, some can be later 'cored' (integrated)
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden }
							is_hun_larp = yes 
						}
						add_claim_by = ROOT 
					}
				
				}
				#Without realism, all claims are immediately cores
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden }
							is_hun_larp = yes 
						}
						add_core_of = ROOT 
					} 		
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = HUN }
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_reassert_old_claims_kingdom_of_hungary
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					CZE = { exists = yes }
					YUG = { exists = yes }
					ROM = { exists = yes }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_little_entente_had_chance_to_awaken } 
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					CZE = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_cze.5 days = 1 } }
					set_global_flag = HUN_little_entente_had_chance_to_awaken
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_little_entente_might_react_defensively
			}
		}

			multiply_temp_variable = {
				var = communism_support
				value = 100
			}
			set_temp_variable = { democratic_support = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { democratic_support = fascism_support }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { democratic_support = communism_support }
			hidden_effect = {
				create_politician_pal_teleki_democratic = yes
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = fascism_support
					communism = communism_support
					democratic = democratic_support
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = HUN_nkp_long name = HUN_nkp }
				set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = HUN_f48_kossuth_long name = HUN_f48_kossuth }
				news_event = { id = hun_news.39 }
			}
		}
	}

		id = HUN_settle_the_matter_of_the_monarchy
		icon = GFX_focus_hun_elect_a_king
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = HUN_dismantle_the_monarchy }
		available = {	
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_the_great_coalition
				has_completed_focus = HUN_align_with_the_victors
				has_completed_focus = HUN_maintain_conservative_government
				has_completed_focus = HUN_promote_hungarism
				has_completed_focus = HUN_gentleman_fascism
			}
		}
		allow_branch = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = HUN_embrace_communism }
		}
		x = 56	#X-ANCHOR (for monarchy branch)
		y = 0
		relative_position_id = HUN_revisionism
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}	
		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL}
		completion_reward = {
			add_political_power = 50
		}
	}
	
	focus = {

			}
		}

		}
	}
